Sun Jan 26 12:56:06 UTC 2025
I compiled wxWidgets with gtk3 and qt5, just as Alien Bob also did,
so I renamed the package from wxgtk to wxwidgets.
wx-gtk2 is not used by any package so much.
Actually wx-qt5 is not used at the moment either,
but it can always be useful to some of you.
While I was at it I added support for Microsoft compression formats, via libmspack.
I also wanted to compile wx-gtk4, but it gives error.
I still used autotools because cmake does not install locales
and does not handle libsuffix well.
